# Weapon flashlight

# Description __

Attaches to a weapon. Provides user with a beam of light. Pressing F (default) to toggle light.

Page views: 7,153  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Holosight

# Description __

A holographic weapon sight with a glowing reticle that increases the accuracy of the weapon and gives a clearer sight picture.

Page views: 6,710  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Weapon Lasersight

# Description __

Attaches to a weapon. Provides user with a guiding laser and reduces weapon sway.

Page views: 6,697  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/weapon.mod.muzzleboost~history)



# Muzzle Boost

# Description __

Increases weapon fire rate by channeling gasses back into the weapon cycling it faster, at the cost of bullet velocity and accuracy.

Page views: 5,434  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Log In](https://auth.facepunch.com/login/?r=aHR0cHM6Ly93aWtpLmZhY2VwdW5jaC5jb20vcnVzdC9pdGVtL3dlYXBvbi5tb2QubXV6emxlYm9vc3Q%3D)
  * [ __Create Account](https://auth.facepunch.com/login/?r=aHR0cHM6Ly93aWtpLmZhY2VwdW5jaC5jb20vcnVzdC9pdGVtL3dlYXBvbi5tb2QubXV6emxlYm9vc3Q%3D)

# Muzzle Brake

# Description __

Lowers recoil felt by the operator but can make bullet path more unpredictable and dealing slightly less damage to your foes.

Page views: 5,269  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

[Home](/rust/) / [Silencer](/rust/item/weapon.mod.silencer)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/weapon.mod.silencer)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/weapon.mod.silencer~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/weapon.mod.silencer~history)



# Silencer

# Description __

Significantly reduces the sound of gunfire, and completely removes any visible muzzle flash at the cost of damage.

Often used when raiding with [explosive ammo](https://wiki.facepunch.com/rust/item/ammo.rifle.explosive) to reduce the chances of a counter-raider hearing the raid. When using a silencer with explosive ammo, the small explosion of the bullet impacting travels further than the gunshot. However, explosive ammo takes a toll on the silencers durability.

Page views: 10,310  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __View](/rust/item/weapon.mod.simplesight)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/weapon.mod.simplesight~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/weapon.mod.simplesight~history)



# Simple Handmade Sight

# Description __

A poorly made sight, slightly better than iron sights.

This sight reduces the change of POV when aiming down sights by 50%. This makes it useful for short range weapons such as shotguns and SMGs but is harder to use at range.

Page views: 6,583  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# 8x Zoom Scope

# Description __

_A small 8x zoom scope._   
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  


# Infomation __

The 8x Zoom Scope is a hand-crafted telescopic sight. Its reticle is simply a thin cross. Its magnification allows for greater precision over long ranges and extending most weapon's range, but is not ideal for close quarter engagements.

# Stats __

  * Accuracy: **+15%**
  * Recoil: **-20%**
  * Zoom: **+8.0x**



# Researching __

  * **2250x** [Scrap](scrap) to go thru the tech tree in a [Work Bench Level 3](workbench3)
  * **125x** [Scrap](scrap) at the [Research Table](research.table)



# Crafting __

  * **50x** [High Quality Metal](metal.refined)



# Recycle __

  * **25x** [High Quality Metal](metal.refined)



# Repair __

Can't be Repaired

# Skins __

  * No

  * [ __View](/rust/item/wiretool)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/wiretool~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/wiretool~history)



# Wire Tool

# Description __

A tool used to make connections between electrical objects. Aim at an object and click on an input/output handle. you can then click on another object's input/output handle to form a connection. holding right mouse will clear or cancel a connection.

Page views: 6,306  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

Spoiled Wolf Meat. Consuming will damage your health.

# Cooked Wolf Meat

# Description __

Cooked Wolf Meat. Eating it will restore some health, hunger, and thirst.

Page views: 2,289  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

Raw Wolf Meat. Eating it will damage your health, try cooking it first.

# Description __

Spoiled Wolf Meat. Consuming will damage your health.

# Wood

# Description __

Wood. Collected from trees and used in many crafting recipes. It's also needed to cook in camp-fires.

Page views: 3,655  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

# Wood Chestplate

# Description __

A shoddy piece of body armor made from Wood and rope.

Page views: 2,461  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Wood Armor Pants

# Description __

A shoddy piece of leg armor made from Wood and rope.

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Work Bench Level 1](/rust/item/workbench1)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/workbench1)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/workbench1~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/workbench1~history)



# Work Bench Level 1

# Description __

This allows you to craft items requiring workbench level 1.

# Crafting __

This item can be crafted anywhere and takes **30** seconds to craft

Quantity | Item  
---|---  
500 | Wood  
100 | Metal Fragments  
50 | Scrap  
  
# Tech Tree __

Press the Use key (Default e) on the Workbench to open the Level 1 Tech Tree

Page views: 94,164  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Work Bench Level 2](/rust/item/workbench2)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/workbench2)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/workbench2~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/workbench2~history)



# Work Bench Level 2

# Description __

_This allows you to craft items requiring workbench level 2_

A [Wood Storage Box](box.wooden) can fit snugly under this Workbench to store commonly used crafting materials. Crafting default blueprint items at this workbench will cut the time by a quarter, and level 1 items by half.

# Crafting __

This item needs to be crafted at a Workbench Level 1 or higher and takes **45** seconds to craft

Quantity | Item  
---|---  
500 | Metal Fragments  
20 | High Quality Metal  
500 | Scrap  
  
# Tech Tree __

Press the Use key (Default e) on the Workbench to open the Level 2 Tech Tree

Page views: 166,366  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/workbench3~history)



# Work Bench Level 3

# Description __

_This allows you to craft items requiring workbench level 3_

A [Wood Storage Box](box.wooden) can fit snugly under this Workbench to store commonly used crafting materials

# Crafting __

This item needs to be crafted at a Workbench Level 2 and takes **60** seconds to craft

Quantity | Item  
---|---  
1000 | Metal Fragments  
100 | High Quality Metal  
1250 | Scrap  
  
# Tech Tree __

Press the Use key (Default e) on the Workbench to open the Level 3 Tech Tree

# Workbench Level 3 Items __

  * [8x Zoom Scope](weapon.mod.small.scope)
  * [Armored Cockpit Vehicle Module]
  * [Armored Door](door.hinged.toptier)
  * [Armored Double Door](door.double.hinged.toptier)
  * [Armored Passenger Vehicle Module]
  * [Assault Rifle](rifle.ak)
  * [Bolt Action Rifle](rifle.bolt)
  * [Explosive 5.56 Rifle Ammo](ammo.rifle.explosive)
  * [Explosives](explosives)

# Festive Doorway Garland

# Description __

A Festive decoration to spruce up your doorway during the holidays! This item requires the Steam Item to be crafted.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x25 Cloth



## Recycling Output __

  * x13 Cloth



Page views: 6,408  
Updated: A Long Time Ago
